           TikTok has struck up licensing deals with all three major record labels. What does this say about the future of the music industry?

           <h3 class="article-name">
            Intels range of more powerful Tiger Lake laptop CPUs gets leaked
           </h3>
           <p class="byline">

              Darren Allan
             </span>
            </span>

            </time>
